<response>{'time': 1518800932915, 'text': 'Thank you for kind review. We will see you soon.'}</response>< Text>
Took my Sapporo girl here, she loved her white miso while I loved my spicy red miso. Naturally, miso broths won't be as creamy and pork fat flavorful as pork broths, so keep that in mind when trying the miso ramen.
Now, for both, generous slices of pork (not one like some cheap ramen shops), with enough noodles and broth to fill you up for lunch for about $10. Really hungry? $15 lunch special with the pork on rice, fried rice, gyoza, etc. Even though we were both hungry and didn't have breakfast, could only finish 75% of the fried rice + pork on rice bowls that came with our ramen.
But, this is not complaining. Fried rice is made well enough that you want to take it home for later, if you didn't already vacuum it up. Lunch special comes with teas, sodas, etc. Iced green tea was just the thing to balance out the spiciness of the red miso ramen (which isn't searing hot thankfully).
Definitely delicious, a place where you just keep eating and eating even if your mind is on something else, and before you know, it's gone! =D
Nice, comfortable spot away from the packed craziness of Sawtelle's ramen shops. Sufficient street parking at meters during the day (only 3, 4 parking spots to the side of the building free). Just remember - same building as the gym! Stay on Olympic and don't turn right (north) like Google Maps accidentally tells you. Service was prompt and attentive for the light crowd, maybe five guests at Thursday lunch.</Text>

<rate>4</rate><Review>Checked this place out (2017/6/10) after driving through Sawtelle on a crowded evening. I wasn't sure what to expect, but am quite glad to have stumbled upon this place!

What I got and what I thought:

Deluxe White Miso Ramen (2017/6/10)
- had a distinct and balanced broth flavor
- solid noodles that could absorb the soup flavor
- thick-cut pork slices that help counter the saltiness
- cabbage (along with the bamboo) help provide a variety of textures
* Something about this dish gives a soothing sense of hominess (beyond the typical ramen experience) and would entice me to come back on a monthly basis or so.

While my dining experience here was somewhat limited, I really enjoyed the food and the quiet atmosphere, and also appreciated the historic timeline of the restaurant mounted on the wall. I am looking forward to future visits to try out the rest of their menu!</Review><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO5DnshF_vInoDq2hm4kB_Xp66H2Hwx48KE1FEO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOIng6AAsbssAXjn2cQ9XAWJ7ls4_0qRdE0mdTU=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><resp>None<//resp><GmapID>0x80c2bb0b7cd824b7:0x6ff9667b2de281f7<//GmapID></record>

Best Panino Sandwich that I ever had in any restaurant. The crunch on the bread was exquisite and the filling of each of the Panini was perfect. We had the classic clubhouse, artichoke, and caprese. My mom and I each ordered a half panino and half soup combo for lunch. They were absolutely delicious, with perfect crusty toasted bread and cheesy fillings. I got the caprese with pesto, mozzarella, and tomatoes, she got the artichoke hearts, mozzarella, and red pepper pesto. Her lentil soup was spicy, hearty, flavorful. I was so sad I couldn‚Äôt really eat any since I am allergic, but I snuck a tiny bite for flavor and paid with a mild allergic reaction (not recommended, but was worth it). I got the tomato soup, which was a nice side to the sandwich. There were several other interesting vegetarian sandwich options, and also a make your own grilled cheese section. I recommend coming here for a delicious filling lunch!

Decor is a bit creepy for me with some scary masks, felt a bit voodoo-esque, but perhaps that is the charm.  Dark, cozy, mysterious. I would not want to be trapped there at night.< /text>

< Text>
This is a long overdue review as we've been going to Mr. Kebab for years! It's the only food my family, some of whom are on keto diet or low carb diet, can agree on. The owners are super friendly and flexible. I love the fact they started doing online orders recently...it makes things super convenient. I sometimes place an order then go to Safeway next door to shop for groceries then pop in at Mr. Kebab to pick up my to go order.

We always get the chicken kebab plate. It comes with salad, 4 chicken skewers, rice and house bread. The combo lamb and beef kofte kebab is also good. It's a lot of food...I always have leftovers for the next day. The meats are always juicy and tender. I'm so glad the combo plate comes with rice because it's soooo good. The salad is always fresh. My kids especially love their garlic fries.

In the years I've been coming to Mr. Kebab, the food has always been good. It's always met my expectations.<//Text>

<review>Whoa!!!!  A small store front looking from outside in, but inside the restaurant was quite a bit of room.  Anyway, I had the sandwich with Chicken.  They grill and rotisserie as Mediterranean Meats are usually cooked.  Mr. Kabob serves Salads (with choice of meat), Kabob's of course, Gyros, Wraps and Sandwhiches called "Doner".  I had their Doner Chicken.

The Bread had some type of seeds cooked into it.  The bread is also very soft with air pockets when taking a bite reminded me of biting into a Marshmallow..  The Chicken was chopped and cooked with sauteed onion.  The Doner sandwhich was topped with Fresh chopped Romaine Lettuce, Tomato and onion and traditional Tzatziki Sauce.  The meal also came with a side salad.

It so happened that the Doner was a little messy than Chicken on a Gyros or a Wrap for that matter, that whatever pieces of Chicken fell on the plate, then used it to top the side Salad and make a Chicken Salad as a second meal.  Delicious!!!   I recommend Mr. Kabob, but will officially give a 4 Star rating because no Military or Veterans discount were recognized.<//review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOD_gXTIAbDiFLKHup5HHbvjy_ixB0xLy9HkyEb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP9K4GA2AEWj9LQPXw5cabc-gSFOOMh5GL5TSSS=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP17_I6xqHH8zFnkoHm6DCK0afsfPD8dE2ei6x0=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNFTrgGMxPY0fJlkUTEUkiEOUaD_s66Bnh4if25=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOvDmH5zS5K9KkBD97aV5XQOVOLJ6XPG98AVZ2a=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO7A3iXZ2xm3eMtHbnljlYtM4aHXSyWUvsin2Va=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN01KXujVRmvlQfIrA3xYtzrlHzmg18e9OI-X3h=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMnr_UOnvxr_D1q6orbTE_d9mFiC7LPNwu5pnqA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNJfNuLO7CwXqWj5oa3y00QwUCU221LRRnlfNyb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOVSwpXc1tTKzPjHKkOozflCbl8SHSLChj7yj4Z=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMXEMkX4dWjoMcPdHKlsmpX8WK4kAXcNkCNPfPg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOsfOScOFfSuRB0Ziddc_eizWNTKZmox8QUIhZZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics><Response>None< /Response><GmapID>0x808f95618c447739:0xb35ef1111ebf6fec<//GmapID></record>

<Text>Food is good and tasty not overly great---2.75 Stars. The meat portions are small, but the prices are also reasonable and the quality is good. The ambience is similar to a nicer Subway. The service can be slow when busy and the staff is friendly. Had the sampler appetizer which I highly recommend as the hummus/tabouli/falafel/dolmas/salad are pretty authentic with good portion sizes. The chicken skewers were dry and very small, but the rice and salad were good. The lamb kebabs were super tiny--think the size of those red n white hard swirl free mints you pick up walking out of the restaurants, however they were tender and nicely seasoned. Would go back for lunch occasionally if craving this style food, but would not make a special trip unless I just happen to be in this area.< /Text></record>

Friendly family restaurant.   I've been there about 4 times now.  I've tried the fallafel plate, the chicken kebab, and the combo with lamb, beef, and chicken. < Review>
I have had two rabbits spayed at this clinic. Both healed well and had no complications. The price is very reasonable especially compared to other exotic animal vets which will charge $300-400 for a rabbit spay. The only reason that I am docking a star is for the following two reasons: 1. it is extremely difficult to get ahold of someone over the phone. Your best bet is to email to get an appointment, 2. the staff is under the false impression that you must fast a rabbit before surgery. DO NOT fast a rabbit prior to surgery it increases their chance of gut stasis and complications. Staff and logistics aside, the surgeon knows what he is doing and I can recommend a rabbit owner to this clinic.<//Review>

<gmapID>0x808561c3cc99e1b1:0x6a8a963fec593186<//gmapID><Date>1622445638158<//Date><resp>None<//resp>< text>
In the world of high end jewelry/watch shopping there's Davidson and Licht and then there's everyone else. From the moment the door is opened for you by a dapper gentleman who smiles and calls your attention to the hand sanitizer, to the champagne/scotch (or chilled bottled water if you prefer) and candied orange slices. This place is pure class without the pretentiousness which usually accompanies multi-million dollar jewelry caches and Rolex/Cartier Authorized Dealer status.

My wife and I spent at least two hours (probably closer to three) poring over various Rolex, Cartier and IWC watches and truly extravagant jewelry. Not once did we feel pressured to purchase. Not once did we encounter the "slickness" all too familiar in high end sales salons. What we did feel was supported and guided through our decision making process. To that end, we owe particular thanks to Orlando, his expertise and his patience. Aside from being a genuine and convivial fellow, it was clearly important to Orlando that our purchase was the right purchase for us. No pressure. No undue urgency tactics. He simply used his knowledge and experience to educate us about what we might like the most and let our preferences lead us from there. Thank you Orlando and thank you Davidson and Licht for a magnificent shopping experience!<//text>

<date>1486426112203<//date>< Review>
Your experience begins with a nice greeting from the door man who will offer to put change in the meter for you. It is always nice to have free parking (back of the store - you just have to ring the bell) Immediately I was greeted by Vince and he became my personal shopping helper. I came in for earrings, specifically the harts on fire collection. The stones are cut so perfectly the light that's comes back out of the diamond shines like no other. You can look through the scope and see how perfectly symmetrical the diamonds are. They are the best cut diamonds in the world, and "Cut" is the most important of the four C's. I was drawn to the 1ct. pair and tried them on. I was sold.
The next day I came back and Vince immediately greeted me again. I wanted to be sure I made the right choice. I tried on a larger more expensive pair and he said they both work but the smaller ones are perfect for everyday wear. He suggested I keep the ones I got. I really appreciated that he didn't up-sell me. Turns out they don't work on commission, how amazing is that; I feel like I can breath unlike at other jewelry stores. Vince made great conversation during the whole experience. He offered to appraise the alexandrite ring I brought in for free. He had me examine my stone with a loop (10x magnifier) and I mentioned that I wish I had one. He helped me out with that too. This has been such a wonderful experience and it gets better! He also steam cleaned my old earrings and new ones. A free service with unlimited visits. I started to talk to Vince about my favorite watch brand Breitling and I asked him to show me some. He brought me over to the section and he pulled out one of the versions I was interested in. Wow, it was beautiful. I just had to get it. In a flash it was on my wrist and fully registered with a 5 yr warranty. He advised me to come in every year or two to get the pressure checked, again free of charge. I brought up a watch winder and he said I'm glad you brought that up, we have a few store models from a vender. He showed me how to use it and put it in my bag. Are you kidding me! It seriously keeps getting better! And Vince was absolutely the best, I would give him a million stars! This jewelry store is by far the best I've ever been in. The cleanliness, the free beverage and snack, the amazing customer service. I would recommend this place to everyone, absolutely the best service you can get. Good buy Tiffany, good buy everywhere else. This is now my go-to jewelry store and look out for Vince. They are all excellent, he is just my personal favorite.< /Review>

We bought a Rolex a number of years ago at their other Walnut Creek location. A few weeks ago we needed to have the band adjusted so we came back. To our surprise it wasn't there. We googled it and walked to the new location.

The new store is beautiful! We walked in with jeans and tennis shoes. We were immediately greeted and helped. While we waited we looked at their large selection of Rolexes. We met Jon Licht, the owner and Jeremiah, the in-house Rolex expert. We learned so much from him about the history of Rolex. Jon has a great sense of humor and gift of gab. We bought two Rolexes! While we were looking they offered to clean our rings and our watches. They cleaned and polished them for free.

We spoke with Jon about our 25th anniversary next year and our desire to have rings made for the special occasion. He put a $100K ring on my wife and walked away. Then I wore it walking around the store. When Jon came back we discussed different possible designs.

We were treated as if we were part of his family. We were not dressed well. We were not wearing a lot of expensive jewelry. We are gay. Sometimes other stores do not give us the time of day, so we just leave and find another store who will treat us with respect. We did not feel this way any time we entered this store.

I highly recommend shopping here.<//text><Pics>None<//Pics><Response>None</Response><GmapID>0x808561c3cc99e1b1:0x6a8a963fec593186<//GmapID></record>
